	focus = {
		id = BBW_ascension_of_rzymkowski
		icon = BBW_ascension_of_rzymkowski
		text_icon = BBW_coalblackmen_focus_style
		prerequisite = { focus = BBW_elderprinzip }
		mutually_exclusive = {
			focus = BBW_ascension_of_zychosiak
		}

		x = -7
		y = 1
		relative_position_id = BBW_elderprinzip
		cost = 2
		
		available = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
				hidden_trigger = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = BBW_rzymkowski_was_ascended_flag } #Flag to prevent AI from taking the focus again after advisor has been replaced}
				}
			}

			has_government = reactionary
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader = {
					ruling_only = yes
					character = BBW_gen_rzymkowski
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = BBW_inner_circle_event_pending_flag
				}
				NOT = { has_country_flag = BBW_inner_circle_event_pending_flag }
			}
		}

		#Focus will need to pause while events are pending
		cancel_if_invalid = no

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INNER_CIRCLE FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL_CHARACTER FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }

		select_effect = { #Necessary to prevent AI from getting stuck if the focus is paused due to available trigger returning false
			set_country_flag = BBW_rzymkowski_ascension_flag
		}

		completion_reward = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = BBW_ascension_of_character_tt
				CHARACTER = BBW_gen_rzymkowski
			}

			custom_effect_tooltip = generic_skip_one_line_tt

			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = BBW_ascension_of_character_focus_tt
				CHARACTER = BBW_gen_rzymkowski
			}

			if = { #Just to make it easy to debug stuff for development
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_1 = 1 }
						check_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_2 = 1 }
						check_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_3 = 1 }
					}
				}
				log = "Advisor was already there. STOP CHEATING!"
			}
			else_if = { # ASCENDED ADVISORS FULL - NEED TO REPLACE SOMEONE
				limit = {
					check_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_1 = 0 compare = not_equals }
					check_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_2 = 0 compare = not_equals }
					check_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_3 = 0 compare = not_equals }
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_variable = { BBW_ascending_advisor = 1 }
					#country_event = BBW_inner_circle.01
				}

				custom_effect_tooltip = generic_skip_one_line_tt
				custom_effect_tooltip = {
					localization_key = BBW_event_to_replace_ascended_advisor_tt
					EVENT = BBW_inner_circle.01.t
					CHARACTER = BBW_gen_rzymkowski
				}
			}
			else = {
				hidden_effect = {
					add_ideas = BBW_rzymkowski_reich_engineer
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_1 = 0 }
					}
					set_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_1 = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_2 = 0 }
					}
					set_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_2 = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_3 = 0 }
					}
					set_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_3 = 1 }
				}
			}

			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = BBW_inner_circle_rzymkowski.01 days = BBW_inner_circle_days_to_start_focus random_days = BBW_inner_circle_random_days }

				clr_country_flag = BBW_rzymkowski_ascension_flag

				#BBW_inner_circle_set_ascension_cd = yes


					set_country_flag = { #Flag to prevent AI from taking the focus again after advisor has been replaced
						flag = BBW_rzymkowski_was_ascended_flag
						days = 1500 # Clear after ~4 years 
						value = 1
					}
			}
		}
	}

			focus = BBW_ascension_of_rzymkowski
		}

		x = 2
		y = 0
		relative_position_id = BBW_ascension_of_rzymkowski
		cost = 2
		
		available = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
				hidden_trigger = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = BBW_zychosiak_was_ascended_flag } #Flag to prevent AI from taking the focus again after advisor has been replaced}
				}
			}

			has_government = reactionary
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader = {
					ruling_only = yes
					character = BBW_zychosiak
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = BBW_inner_circle_event_pending_flag
				}
				NOT = { has_country_flag = BBW_inner_circle_event_pending_flag }
			}

		}

		#Focus will need to pause while events are pending
		cancel_if_invalid = no

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INNER_CIRCLE FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL_CHARACTER FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }

		select_effect = { #Necessary to prevent AI from getting stuck if the focus is paused due to available trigger returning false
			set_country_flag = BBW_zychosiak_ascension_flag
		}

		completion_reward = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = BBW_ascension_of_character_tt
				CHARACTER = BBW_zychosiak
			}

			custom_effect_tooltip = generic_skip_one_line_tt

			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = BBW_ascension_of_character_focus_tt
				CHARACTER = BBW_zychosiak
			}

			if = { #Just to make it easy to debug stuff for development
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_1 = 2 }
						check_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_2 = 2 }
						check_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_3 = 2 }
					}
				}
				log = "Advisor was already there. STOP CHEATING!"
			}
			else_if = { # ASCENDED ADVISORS FULL - NEED TO REPLACE SOMEONE
				limit = {
					check_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_1 = 0 compare = not_equals }
					check_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_2 = 0 compare = not_equals }
					check_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_3 = 0 compare = not_equals }
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_variable = { BBW_ascending_advisor = 2 }
					#country_event = BBW_inner_circle.01
				}

				custom_effect_tooltip = generic_skip_one_line_tt
				custom_effect_tooltip = {
					localization_key = BBW_event_to_replace_ascended_advisor_tt
					EVENT = BBW_inner_circle.01.t
					CHARACTER = BBW_zychosiak
				}
			}
			else = {
				hidden_effect = {
					add_ideas = BBW_zychosiak_reich_architect
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_1 = 0 }
					}
					set_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_1 = 2 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_2 = 0 }
					}
					set_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_2 = 2 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_3 = 0 }
					}
					set_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_3 = 2 }
				}
			}

			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = BBW_inner_circle_zychosiak.01 days = BBW_inner_circle_days_to_start_focus random_days = BBW_inner_circle_random_days }
				clr_country_flag = BBW_zychosiak_ascension_flag

				#BBW_inner_circle_set_ascension_cd = yes
				
				set_country_flag = { #Flag to prevent AI from taking the focus again after advisor has been replaced
					flag = BBW_zychosiak_was_ascended_flag
					days = 1500 # Clear after ~4 years 
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}

					character = BBW_gen_janecki
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = BBW_inner_circle_event_pending_flag
				}
				NOT = { has_country_flag = BBW_inner_circle_event_pending_flag }
			}

		}

		#Focus will need to pause while events are pending
		cancel_if_invalid = no

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INNER_CIRCLE FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL_CHARACTER FOCUS_FILTER_MANPOWER }

		select_effect = { #Necessary to prevent AI from getting stuck if the focus is paused due to available trigger returning false
			set_country_flag = BBW_janecki_ascension_flag
		}

		completion_reward = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = BBW_ascension_of_character_tt
				CHARACTER = BBW_gen_janecki
			}
			
			custom_effect_tooltip = generic_skip_one_line_tt

			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = BBW_ascension_of_character_focus_tt
				CHARACTER = BBW_gen_janecki
			}

			if = { #Just to make it easy to debug stuff for development
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_1 = 4 }
						check_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_2 = 4 }
						check_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_3 = 4 }
					}
				}
				log = "Advisor was already there. STOP CHEATING!"
			}
			else_if = { # ASCENDED ADVISORS FULL - NEED TO REPLACE SOMEONE
				limit = {
					check_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_1 = 0 compare = not_equals }
					check_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_2 = 0 compare = not_equals }
					check_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_3 = 0 compare = not_equals }
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_variable = { BBW_ascending_advisor = 4 }
					#country_event = BBW_inner_circle.01 #Replace Advisor
				}

				custom_effect_tooltip = generic_skip_one_line_tt
				custom_effect_tooltip = {
					localization_key = BBW_event_to_replace_ascended_advisor_tt
					EVENT = BBW_inner_circle.01.t
					CHARACTER = BBW_gen_janecki
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = generic_skip_one_line_tt

				#country_event = BBW_inner_circle_janecki.00 #Pick Himmler's branch (Can only be fired once)
				
				hidden_effect = {
					add_ideas = BBW_janecki_chief_of_german_police
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_1 = 0 }
					}
					set_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_1 = 4 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_2 = 0 }
					}
					set_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_2 = 4 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_3 = 0 }
					}
					set_variable = { BBW_ascended_advisor_3 = 4 }
				}
			}

			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = BBW_inner_circle_janecki.01 days = BBW_inner_circle_days_to_start_focus random_days = BBW_inner_circle_random_days }
				clr_country_flag = BBW_janecki_ascension_flag

				#BBW_inner_circle_set_ascension_cd = yes

				set_country_flag = { #Flag to prevent AI from taking the focus again after advisor has been replaced
					flag = BBW_janecki_was_ascended_flag
					days = 1500 # Clear after ~4 years 
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
